IN THIS FILE "datatype=MIXED(PROTEIN: 1-2049, DNA: 2050-6730)" WITH datatype= PROTEIN.  This is not true but this trick will let you hopen the file in PAUP.IN PAUP EXECUTE THE FOLLOWING COMMANDS:DELETE Dictyostelium; EXLCUDE nuc;EXPORT FILE = ERWIN_ET_AL_CLOCK_DATASET.NEX FORMAT=NEXUS;THE ERWIN_ET_AL_CLOCK_DATASET.NEX IS THE FILE WE USED FOR THE MOLECULAR CLOCK ANALYSES.JUSTIFICATIONS FOR NOT USING THE rRNA DATA IN THE MOLECULAR CLOCK ANALYSES IS REPORTED IN THE SOM METHODS.WE DID NOT USE Dictyostelium AS AN OUTGROUP IN THE CLOCK ANALYSES BECAUSE THERE IS NO EVIDENCE THAT CAN BE USED TO DEFINE A ROOT-PRIOR AGE IF Dictyostelium IS USED AS THE OUTGROUP (I.E. DICTYOSTELIUM VS. FUNGI+HOLOZIA SPLIT AGE IS NOT KNOWN).WHEN DICTOSTELYUM IS NOT INCLUDED IN THE DATA SET THE OUTGROUP BECOME THE FUNGI AND A PRIOR ROOT AGE FOR THE FUNGI-HOLOZOA SPLIT IS AVAILABLE - SEE SOM.]
